             <h3 class="title">
              <a href="/news/1-hospitalized-following-shooting-at-sarasota-county-fairgrounds">
               Sarasota police increase security after 18-year-old shot at county fair
              </a>
             </h3>
            </header>
            <p>
             An 18-year-old male was seriously injured Saturday night after being shot at the Sarasota County Fairgrounds shortly after 10 p.m., according to the Sarasota Police Department.

               </a>
              </h3>
             </header>
